################################################################
#  EMM INPUT DATA FILE: EMMCNTL
#
#  FORMAT RULES:
#  ALL DATA IS CONTAINED IN COLUMNS 1-132
#  DATA COLUMNS MUST BE SEPARATED BY 1+ SPACE
#  CHARACTER DATA MUST BE ENCLOSED IN ' '
#  DATA LINES MAY BE COMMENTED OUT OR SKIPPED BY ROUTINE
#  LINES BEGINNING WITH # ARE COMMENTS AND % ARE TABLE HEADERS
#  OTHERWISE LINE IS A DATA RECORD IN A DATA TABLE
#  LEAVE COLUMN 1 IN DATA ROWS BLANK TO ALLOW INSERTION OF # (NOT REQ'D)
#
################################################################
%SCENARIO  %
####            UFSCEN
'SCENARIO NAME' 'BASE'
%RPT/DBG SW%
### IN OUT PLT CRV DBG SO2 LD TMP RP FL ETTIN ETTDF ETT CNCT ETDM RP2 MC
'SW' 9  10  11  12   1  14 15  16 17 18     1     0   1    1    1   1  1
%OUT LCV SW%
#### ULCVSW : (=1) PRINT EFD LOAD CURVES TO EMMPRNT, OTHERWISE NO
####
 'ULCVSW' 0
%EMMDB SW  %
#### USW_DBS: USER SWITCH TO DETERMINE LEVEL OF OUTPUT TO EMM DATABASE
###   0=NO DATABASE PRINTS,1=NO PLANT FILE PRINTS,2=WITH PLANT FILE PRINTS
 'USW_DBS'  2
%DAF/CORE S%
####    USW_DISP USW_BILD USW_EIJ USW_ETTDF
'DAF SW'       0        0       0         0
%NUM BLOCKS%
####   LAST_STEO_YR EX_COAL NW_COAL UZ_PLT UZ_ETT
'#BLKS'      15        6      12      6     23
%FUEL P TOL%
####           UFPTOL
'FUEL PR TOL'  0.15
%ETT SWITCH%
####  USW_CANACC:  allow the acceleration of canadian projects, 0 = no, 1 = yes
####                  USW_ETT USW_XP  USW_CANACC
'USW ETT,XP,canacc'       1      0        0
%LOAD CR SW%
####          USW_LDC   0 = NERC,  1 = LDSM
'LC SW'    1
%OVERWRITE SW%
####          USW_OVER   0 = NO,  1 = HIST,  2 = HIST & STEO
'OVR SW'          1
%REFURB%
####          URFURB                 UFACPS     UFACP2
'HEATRATE FACTOR'         0.05        1.20       0.96
%OWNERSHIP SW%
####          USW_OWN
'OWN SW'         4
%EFD MAINTENANCE SW%
####          USW_PM  (0=EFD, 1=ECP)
'PM SW'          0
%DS PARAMS %
#### N_STO_INC                   - Number_Storage_Increments
#### hoursToBuy                  - Diurnal storage duration of discharge
#### hoursToSell                 - Diurnal storage duration needed for charging
#### Battery_Extra_Discount      - Diurnal storage capacity extra discount rate for future arbitrage value
#### batteryEfficiency           - Diurnal storage effiency
#### Battery_Initial_Percent     - Diurnal storage initial percentage rate for determining incremental battery size as a function of regional peak load value
#### Battery_Incremental_Percent - Diurnal storage incremental percentage rate for determining incremental battery size as a function of regional peak load value
#### Battery_Maximum_Percent     - Diurnal storage maximum percentage rate for determining incremental battery size as a function of regional peak load value
  1 4 4 0.000 0.85 0.01 0.01 0.05
%FUEL PR SW%
####                     USW_NERC USW_CENS USW_GASR USW_CLRG
'USW NERC,CENS,GASR,CLRG'       0        0        0        0
%EXEC YEARS%
####   UHBSYR: HISTORICAL BASE YEAR
####   UESTYR: INITIAL EXECUTION YEAR FOR EMM AND RENEW
####   UISTYR: INITIAL INPUT YEAR FOR EMM DATA
####   UPSTYR: INITIAL EXECUTION YEAR FOR ECP (NO LONGER SET TO ECP_FYR IN UDAT)
####   UPLRYR: INITIAL YEAR TO START LEARNING (NO LONGER SET TO ECP_FYR - 1 IN UDAT)
####   EFPSYR: BASE YEAR FOR EFP FINANCIAL DATA INPUTS
####         UHBSYR  UESTYR  UISTYR  UPSTYR  ULRSYR   EFPSYR
'EXEC YEARS'   1989    2010    2000    2022    2019     2011
%NUM OF YRS%
####          UNYEAR (MUST BE .LE. MNUMYR, CURRENTLY 46 = 2035)
'NUM OF YRS'    61
%NO CAIR YEAR%
####   UYR_NOCAIR: YEAR TO TURN OFF CAIR IN EFD/CMM (0 = Leave intact)
####   UYR_RSCAIR: YEAR TO RESUME CAIR AFTER CSAPR (0 = Never)
####          UYR_NOCAIR      UYR_RSCAIR
'NOCAIR YR'      2015               0

'MRUN YEAR'        9999         9999        2020        2025

####           CO2_STDSW - Switch to Indicate State Grouping (0=No Std,1=No longer active,2=No longer active,3=EMM)
####           CO2_STDBY - Year Data to Use for State Grouping of Standards
####           CO2_STDWT - Switch to Indicate State Group WGT (0=None,1=Hist Gen, 2=Hist Dem, 3=EMM Affected Gen, 4 = EMM Total Gen)
####           CO2_HRTSW - Switch to Include Heat Rate Improvements (0=No,1=Yes)
####           CO2_EFFSW - Switch to Include Efficiency Rate Improvements (0=No,1=Yes)
####           CO2_STDPH - Switch to Phase in 1st few years of Intensity Standards (0=No,1=Alternate Phase 1,2=Alternate Phase 2,etc)
####           CO2_STDQT - Switch for Type of Quantity Limit (0=Original Rule Existing Capacity,1=Original Rule Existing/New,2=Final Rule Existing,3=Final Rule Ex/New)
####           CO2_EORSW - Switch to turn off CO2 for EOR (0=No,1=Yes)
####           CO2_PRCSW - Switch to Indicate pricing methodology (0=no adder, 1=EFD prc, 2=ECP prc, 3= diff (ECP-EFD), 4= adder for new affected)
####           CO2_ECPSW - Switch to Indicate ECP price to use (1=ECP year 2, 2=ECP levelized)
####           CO2_TRDSW - Switch to Include Interregional Trade in Intensity Standard (0=No,1=Yes)
####           CO2_ERCSW - Switch to Include ERC Supply Curve in Final CPP (0=No,1=Yes)
####           CO2_ERCPR - Switch for CPP ERC Pricing (0=None, 1=EFD, 2=ECP 1yr, 3=ECP lev)
####           CO2_ENDCG - Switch to Include End-Use RNW in rate-base calculation (0=No, 1=Yes)
####           CO2_STDSW   CO2_STDBY   CO2_STDWT   CO2_HRTSW   CO2_EFFSW   CO2_STDPH   CO2_STDQT   CO2_EORSW  CO2_PRCSW  CO2_ECPSW  CO2_TRDSW  CO2_ERCSW  CO2_ERCPR  CO2_ENDCG

%ECP TECH  %
#### Technologies used for ECP builds
#### UPLNTCD : 2 Character Plant Codes
#### UPLNAME : Long Plant Names
#### UPLTISW: Used to determine if technology is being used
####          (not currently used)
#### UCPDSPIS: Used to determine if tech is dispatchable (DSP)
#### UCPINTIS: Used to determine if tech is intermittent renewable (INT)
#### UCPRNWIS: Used to determine if tech is non-int renewable (RNW)
#### UCPDGNIS: Used to determine if tech is distributed generation (DGN)
#### UCPSTOIS: Used to determine if tech is storage (STO)
#### UCPFTABI: Used to map technology to FTAB Table 9 category
#### UCPVSTOR: Used to map technology to Value of Storage category
#### UECP_HTRT_ADJ: Converts Heatrate to Unscrubbed / UnCarbon Capture Heatrate
#### UECP_CPEN_ADJ: Converts O&M costs UnCarbon Capture O&M costs
#### ALT_UECP_CPEN_ADJ: Converts O&M costs UnCarbon Capture O&M costs with minimum capture
#### NO_CCS_PLTCD: Plant code of non-CCS plant that corresponds to a plant with Capture

#### HG_BYR  - Year Banks Can Start to be Accumulated

%HG EMF INFO%
####
#### Mercury Emissions Factors and ACI Info
#### Column  1 - ECP Code
#### Column  2 - ECP Index
#### Column  3 - PLNT_EMF(ECPt,1)  - Mercury EMF - Bituminous
#### Column  4 - PLNT_EMF(ECPt,2)  - Mercury EMF - Subbituminous
#### Column  5 - PLNT_EMF(ECPt,3)  - Mercury EMF - Lignite
#### Column  6 - ACI_STEPS(ECPt,1) - Number of ACI Steps to Create - Bituminous
#### Column  7 - ACI_STEPS(ECPt,2) - Number of ACI Steps to Create - Subbituminous
#### Column  8 - ACI_STEPS(ECPt,3) - Number of ACI Steps to Create - Lignite
#### Column  9 - HG_CHOICE(ECPt)   - Choice of Input or Output Mercury Standard: 0=>None, 1=>Input, 2=>Output, 3=>Either
#### Column 10 - HG_CLASS(ECPt)    - Mercury Compliance Class: 0=>NA, 1=>Existing, 2=>New PC, 3=>IGCC Other
#### Column 11 - MIN_EMF(ECPt,1)   - Minimum Mercury EMF achievable with ACI - Bituminous
#### Column 12 - MIN_EMF(ECPt,2)   - Minimum Mercury EMF achievable with ACI - Subbituminous
#### Column 13 - MIN_EMF(ECPt,3)   - Minimum Mercury EMF achievable with ACI - Lignite
#### Column 14 - ACI_FOM_SW(ECPt)  - Activated Carbon Code 2=> Include Capital Costs and Fixed O&M in Operates 1=> Just Variable Costs in Operates
#### Column 15 - ACI_OandM(ECPt,1) - Incremental O&M for ACI - Bituminous (87$/MWh)
#### Column 16 - ACI_OandM(ECPt,2) - Incremental O&M for ACI - Subbituminous (87$/MWh)
#### Column 17 - ACI_OandM(ECPt,3) - Incremental O&M for ACI - Lignite (87$/MWh)
####
####  ECP ECP       PLNT_EMF      ACI_STEPS HG HG       MIN_EMF      FOM      ACI_OandM
#### CODE INDX    BIT   SUB   LIG   B S L   CH CL   BIT   SUB   LIG   SW    BIT   SUB   LIG
####
